ase_stockpile_market_volume_records_aeroplanes = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_variable = ase_stockpile_market_volume_aeroplanes
        }
        value = var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_aeroplanes
        if = {
            limit = {
                var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_aeroplanes >= 0.10
            }
            modulo = {
                value = var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_aeroplanes
                multiply = 10
                floor = yes
                divide = 10
            }
        }
        multiply = 100
        add = 1
    }
    else = {
        value = 0
    }
}

ase_stockpile_market_volume_average_aeroplanes = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_variable = ase_stockpile_market_volume_aeroplanes
        }
        value = var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_aeroplanes
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_local_variable = ase_stockpile_market_volume_records
            }
            divide = local_var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_records
        }
        else = {
            divide = ase_stockpile_market_volume_records_aeroplanes
        }
        multiply = 10
        round = yes
        divide = 10
    }
    else = {
        value = market.mg:aeroplanes.market_goods_sell_orders
        multiply = ase_stockpile_reserve_target_sell_factor
        add = {
            value = market.mg:aeroplanes.market_goods_buy_orders
            multiply = ase_stockpile_reserve_target_buy_factor
        }
    }
}

    else = {
        value = market.mg:wine.market_goods_sell_orders
        multiply = ase_stockpile_reserve_target_sell_factor
        add = {
            value = market.mg:wine.market_goods_buy_orders
            multiply = ase_stockpile_reserve_target_buy_factor
        }
    }
}

ase_stockpile_market_volume_records_wood = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_variable = ase_stockpile_market_volume_wood
        }
        value = var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_wood
        if = {
            limit = {
                var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_wood >= 0.10
            }
            modulo = {
                value = var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_wood
                multiply = 10
                floor = yes
                divide = 10
            }
        }
        multiply = 100
        add = 1
    }
    else = {
        value = 0
    }
}

ase_stockpile_market_volume_average_wood = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_variable = ase_stockpile_market_volume_wood
        }
        value = var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_wood
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_local_variable = ase_stockpile_market_volume_records
            }
            divide = local_var:ase_stockpile_market_volume_records
        }
        else = {
            divide = ase_stockpile_market_volume_records_wood
        }
        multiply = 10
        round = yes
        divide = 10
    }
    else = {
        value = market.mg:wood.market_goods_sell_orders
        multiply = ase_stockpile_reserve_target_sell_factor
        add = {
            value = market.mg:wood.market_goods_buy_orders
            multiply = ase_stockpile_reserve_target_buy_factor
        }
    }
}

ase_stockpile_country_price_target_saving_oil = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            is_player = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_variable = ase_stockpile_country_price_target_saving_oil
            }
            value = var:ase_stockpile_country_price_target_saving_oil
        }
        else = {
            value = ase_stockpile_price_target_saving_default
        }
    }
    else = {
        value = -0.10
        if = {
            limit = {
                ase_stockpile_goods_priority_oil <= 10
            }
            subtract = 0.05
            if = {
                limit = {
                    ase_stockpile_goods_priority_oil <= 8
                }
                subtract = 0.05
                if = {
                    limit = {
                        ase_stockpile_goods_priority_oil <= 7
                    }
                    subtract = 0.05
                    if = {
                        limit = {
                            ase_stockpile_goods_priority_oil <= 6
                        }
                        subtract = 0.05
                        
                        if = {
                            limit = {
                                ase_stockpile_goods_priority_oil <= 5
                            }
                            subtract = 0.05
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

    min = ase_stockpile_country_price_target_saving_min
    max = ase_stockpile_country_price_target_saving_max
}

ase_stockpile_country_price_target_spending_oil = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            is_player = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_variable = ase_stockpile_country_price_target_spending_oil
            }
            value = var:ase_stockpile_country_price_target_spending_oil
        }
        else = {
            value = ase_stockpile_price_target_spending_default
        }
    }
    else = {
        value = 0.10
        if = {
            limit = {
                ase_stockpile_goods_priority_oil <= 8
            }
            add = 0.05
            if = {
                limit = {
                    ase_stockpile_goods_priority_oil <= 4
                }
                add = 0.05
            }
        }
    }

    min = ase_stockpile_country_price_target_spending_min
    max = ase_stockpile_country_price_target_spending_max
}

ase_stockpile_market_reserve_aeroplanes = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            has_variable = ase_stockpile_market_reserve_aeroplanes
        }
        value = var:ase_stockpile_market_reserve_aeroplanes
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            this = market.owner
        }
        value = ase_stockpile_country_reserve_aeroplanes
    }
    else = {
        value = 0
    }
}

ase_stockpile_market_reserve_target_aeroplanes = {
    value = ase_stockpile_market_volume_average_aeroplanes
    divide = 10
    multiply = ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_target_aeroplanes
}

ase_stockpile_market_to_max_reserve_aeroplanes = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            ase_stockpile_market_reserve_aeroplanes = 0
        }
        value = 0
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            ase_stockpile_market_reserve_target_aeroplanes = 0
        }
        value = 1
    }
    else = {
        value = ase_stockpile_market_reserve_aeroplanes
        divide = ase_stockpile_market_reserve_target_aeroplanes
        min = 0
    }
}

ase_stockpile_market_reserve_limit_aeroplanes = {
    value = ase_stockpile_market_volume_average_aeroplanes
    divide = 10
    multiply = 52
    multiply = ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_max_factor_aeroplanes
    multiply = 2.00
    min = 20
}

        limit = {
            ase_stockpile_market_reserve_luxury_clothes = 0
        }
        value = 0
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            ase_stockpile_market_reserve_target_luxury_clothes = 0
        }
        value = 1
    }
    else = {
        value = ase_stockpile_market_reserve_luxury_clothes
        divide = ase_stockpile_market_reserve_target_luxury_clothes
        min = 0
    }
}

ase_stockpile_market_reserve_limit_luxury_clothes = {
    value = ase_stockpile_market_volume_average_luxury_clothes
    divide = 10
    multiply = 52
    multiply = ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_max_factor_luxury_clothes
    multiply = 2.00
    min = 20
}

            ase_stockpile_market_reserve_tea = 0
        }
        value = 0
    }
    else_if = {
        limit = {
            ase_stockpile_market_reserve_target_tea = 0
        }
        value = 1
    }
    else = {
        value = ase_stockpile_market_reserve_tea
        divide = ase_stockpile_market_reserve_target_tea
        min = 0
    }
}

ase_stockpile_market_reserve_limit_tea = {
    value = ase_stockpile_market_volume_average_tea
    divide = 10
    multiply = 52
    multiply = ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_max_factor_tea
    multiply = 2.00
    min = 20
}

ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_target_aeroplanes = {
    value = 52
    multiply = ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_target_factor_aeroplanes
}

ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_target_factor_aeroplanes = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            is_player = yes
        }
        if = {
            limit = {
                has_variable = ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_target_factor_aeroplanes
            }
            value = var:ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_target_factor_aeroplanes
        }
        else = {
            value = ase_stockpile_goods_reserve_max_factor_aeroplanes
            multiply = ase_stockpile_player_reserve_weeks_target_factor
        }
    }
    else = {
        value = 1
        multiply = ase_stockpile_goods_reserve_weeks_max_factor
    }

    multiply = 4
    round = yes
    divide = 4

    min = 0.25
    max = ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_max_factor_aeroplanes
}

ase_stockpile_country_reserve_weeks_max_factor_aeroplanes = {
    if = {
        limit = {
            ase_stockpile_goods_reserve_max_factor_aeroplanes = 1
        }
        value = ase_stockpile_goods_reserve_weeks_max_factor
    }
    else = {
        value = ase_stockpile_goods_reserve_max_factor_aeroplanes
        multiply = ase_stockpile_goods_reserve_weeks_max_factor

        multiply = 4
        round = yes
        divide = 4

        min = 0.25
        max = 2.00
    }
}

            }

                value = 0.75
                if = {

                    }
                    subtract = 0.25
                }

                    limit = {

                    }
                    subtract = 0.25
                }
            }
        }
        multiply = ase_stockpile_goods_reserve_weeks_max_factor
    }

    multiply = 4
    round = yes
